  IF(AND(GT(NUM0, ?a), EQ(MOD(?b, ?a), NUM0)), MUL(MAX(?x, MUL(?y, DIV(?b, ?a))), ?a), MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))) -> MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))
  IF(AND(GT(?a, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?b, ?a), NUM0)), MUL(MIN(?x, MUL(?y, DIV(?b, ?a))), ?a), MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))) -> MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), MUL(?y, ?b))
  IF(AND(GT(?b, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?a, ?b), NUM0)), PLUS(MUL(?x, DIV(?a, ?b)), DIV(?y, ?b)), DIV(PLUS(MUL(?x, ?a), ?y), ?b)) -> DIV(PLUS(MUL(?x, ?a), ?y), ?b)
  IF(AND(GT(NUM0, ?a), EQ(MOD(?b, ?a), NUM0)), MUL(MAX(?x, DIV(?b, ?a)), ?a), MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)) -> MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)
  IF(AND(GT(?a, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?b, ?a), NUM0)), MUL(MIN(?x, DIV(?b, ?a)), ?a), MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)) -> MIN(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)
  IF(AND(GT(?b, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?a, ?b), NUM0)), PLUS(DIV(?x, ?b), DIV(?a, ?b)), DIV(PLUS(?x, ?a), ?b)) -> DIV(PLUS(?x, ?a), ?b)
  IF(AND(NE(?c1, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?c0, ?c1), NUM0)), MOD(?y, ?c1), MOD(PLUS(MUL(?x, ?c0), ?y), ?c1)) -> MOD(PLUS(MUL(?x, ?c0), ?y), ?c1)
  IF(AND(GT(?b, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?a, ?b), NUM0)), MUL(?x, DIV(?a, ?b)), DIV(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)) -> DIV(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)
  IF(AND(GT(?a, NUM0), EQ(MOD(?b, ?a), NUM0)), DIV(?x, DIV(?b, ?a)), DIV(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)) -> DIV(MUL(?x, ?a), ?b)
  IF(IS_CONST_NEG(?c0), GT(?x, MIN(?z, PLUS(?y, ?c0))), GT(MIN(?x, ?y), MIN(?z, PLUS(?y, ?c0)))) -> GT(MIN(?x, ?y), MIN(?z, PLUS(?y, ?c0)))
  IF(IS_CONST_POS(?c0), GT(?x, MAX(?z, PLUS(?y, ?c0))), GT(MAX(?x, ?y), MAX(?z, PLUS(?y, ?c0)))) -> GT(MAX(?x, ?y), MAX(?z, PLUS(?y, ?c0)))
  IF(IS_CONST_POS(?z), GT(?x, MINUS(MUL(PLUS(?y, NUM1), ?z), NUM1)), GT(DIV(?x, ?z), ?y)) -> GT(DIV(?x, ?z), ?y)
  IF(IS_CONST_POS(?y), GT(DIV(MINUS(PLUS(?z, ?y), NUM1), ?y), ?x), GT(?z, MUL(?x, ?y))) -> GT(?z, MUL(?x, ?y))
  IF(IS_CONST_POS(?c0), GT(?x, MIN(?z, ?y)), GT(MIN(?x, PLUS(?y, ?c0)), MIN(?z, ?y))) -> GT(MIN(?x, PLUS(?y, ?c0)), MIN(?z, ?y))
  IF(IS_CONST_NEG(?c0), GT(?x, MAX(?z, ?y)), GT(MAX(?x, PLUS(?y, ?c0)), MAX(?z, ?y))) -> GT(MAX(?x, PLUS(?y, ?c0)), MAX(?z, ?y))
